\DoxyCodeLine{694   \textcolor{comment}{// Handle code flushing time deltas. Times are incremented conservatively:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695   \textcolor{comment}{// 1. The first delta is 0s.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696   \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Any delta is rounded downwards to a full second.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697   \textcolor{comment}{// 3. 0s-\/deltas are carried over to the next GC with their precise diff. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{698   \textcolor{comment}{//    allows for frequent GCs (within a single second) to be attributed}}
